[Bug] Compiler panic in SSA const propagation: `ParseIntError { kind: PosOverflow }` on element write to array of size > 256 with `u8` index
The compiler panics with `Parsing guarantees this works.: ParseIntError { kind: PosOverflow }` in [`ast/src/const_eval/evaluate.rs` `literal_to_value`](https://github.com/ProvableHQ/leo/blob/7e6b2a1ad7/crates/ast/src/const_eval/evaluate.rs) when an array element write `t[i] = v` is performed on an array whose length exceeds 256 and the index `i` is typed `u8`. The SSA const propagation pass synthesizes a literal in the index type whose value cannot be represented in `u8`.

MRE:
```leo
program test.aleo {
    fn foo(t: [u8; 257]) -> [u8; 257] {
        t[0u8] = 1u8;
        return t;
    }
}
```

Reproduce: create a minimal `program.json` (`"program": "test.aleo"`), save the MRE as `src/main.leo`, run `leo build`.

```

note: run with `RUST_BACKTRACE=1` environment variable to display a backtrace
```

    38	impl Value {
    39	    /// Are the values equal, according to SnarkVM?
    40	    ///
    41	    /// We use this rather than the Eq trait so we can
    42	    /// fail when comparing values of different types,
    43	    /// rather than just returning false.
    44	    pub fn eq(&self, rhs: &Self) -> Result<bool> {
    45	        if self.id != rhs.id {
    46	            return Ok(false);
    47	        }
    48	        use ValueVariants::*;
    49	        Ok(match (&self.contents, &rhs.contents) {
    50	            (Unsuffixed(..), _) | (_, Unsuffixed(..)) => halt_no_span2!("Error"),
    51	            (Unit, Unit) => true,
    52	            (Tuple(x), Tuple(y)) => {
    53	                if x.len() != y.len() {
    54	                    return Ok(false);
    55	                }
    56	                for (x0, y0) in x.iter().zip(y) {
    57	                    if !x0.eq(y0)? {
    58	                        return Ok(false);
    59	                    }
    60	                }
    61	                true
    62	            }
    63	            (Svm(x), Svm(y)) => x == y,
    64	            (_, _) => halt_no_span2!("Type failure"),
    65	        })
    66	    }
    67	
    68	    /// Resolves an unsuffixed literal to a typed `Value` using the provided optional `Type`. If the value is unsuffixed
    69	    /// and a type is provided, parses the string into the corresponding `Value` variant. Handles integers of various
    70	    /// widths and special types like `Field`, `Group`, and `Scalar`. If no type is given or the value is already typed,
    71	    /// returns the original value. Returns an error if type inference is not possible or parsing fails.
    72	    pub fn resolve_if_unsuffixed(&self, ty: &Option<Type>, span: Span) -> Result<Value> {
    73	        if let ValueVariants::Unsuffixed(s) = &self.contents {
    74	            if let Some(ty) = ty {
    75	                let value = match ty {
    76	                    Type::Integer(IntegerType::U8) => {
    77	                        let s = s.replace("_", "");

    79	                    }

    81	                        let s = s.replace("_", "");
    82	                        u16::from_str_by_radix(&s).expect("Parsing guarantees this works.").into()

    94	                        u128::from_str_by_radix(&s).expect("Parsing guarantees this works.").into()

    97	                        let s = s.replace("_", "");
    98	                        i8::from_str_by_radix(&s).expect("Parsing guarantees this works.").into()
    99	                    }
   100	                    Type::Integer(IntegerType::I16) => {

   102	                        i16::from_str_by_radix(&s).expect("Parsing guarantees this works.").into()
   103	                    }

   139	pub fn literal_to_value(literal: &Literal, expected_ty: &Option<Type>) -> Result<Value> {
   140	    Ok(match &literal.variant {
   141	        LiteralVariant::Address(s) => {
   142	            if s.ends_with(".aleo") {
   143	                let program_id: ProgramID<CurrentNetwork> = s.parse()?;
   144	                program_id.to_address()?.into()
   145	            } else {
   146	                let address: Address = s.parse().expect_tc(literal.span)?;
   147	                address.into()
   148	            }
   149	        }
   150	        LiteralVariant::Boolean(b) => (*b).into(),
   151	        LiteralVariant::Field(s) => {
   152	            SvmLiteralParam::Field(prepare_snarkvm_string(s, "field").parse().expect_tc(literal.span)?).into()
   153	        }
   154	        LiteralVariant::Group(s) => {
   155	            SvmLiteralParam::Group(prepare_snarkvm_string(s, "group").parse().expect_tc(literal.span)?).into()
   156	        }
   157	
   158	        LiteralVariant::Identifier(s) => {
   159	            let identifier = SvmIdentifierLiteral::new(s).expect_tc(literal.span)?;
   160	            SvmLiteralParam::Identifier(Box::new(identifier)).into()
   161	        }
   162	        LiteralVariant::Integer(IntegerType::U8, s, ..) => {
   163	            let s = s.replace("_", "");
   164	            u8::from_str_by_radix(&s).expect("Parsing guarantees this works.").into()
   165	        }
   166	        LiteralVariant::Integer(IntegerType::U16, s, ..) => {
   167	            let s = s.replace("_", "");
   168	            u16::from_str_by_radix(&s).expect("Parsing guarantees this works.").into()
   169	        }
   170	        LiteralVariant::Integer(IntegerType::U32, s, ..) => {
   171	            let s = s.replace("_", "");
   172	            u32::from_str_by_radix(&s).expect("Parsing guarantees this works.").into()
   173	        }
   174	        LiteralVariant::Integer(IntegerType::U64, s, ..) => {
   175	            let s = s.replace("_", "");
   176	            u64::from_str_by_radix(&s).expect("Parsing guarantees this works.").into()
   177	        }
   178	        LiteralVariant::Integer(IntegerType::U128, s, ..) => {
   179	            let s = s.replace("_", "");
   180	            u128::from_str_by_radix(&s).expect("Parsing guarantees this works.").into()
   181	        }
   182	        LiteralVariant::Integer(IntegerType::I8, s, ..) => {
   183	            let s = s.replace("_", "");
   184	            i8::from_str_by_radix(&s).expect("Parsing guarantees this works.").into()
   185	        }
   186	        LiteralVariant::Integer(IntegerType::I16, s, ..) => {
   187	            let s = s.replace("_", "");
   188	            i16::from_str_by_radix(&s).expect("Parsing guarantees this works.").into()
   189	        }
   190	        LiteralVariant::Integer(IntegerType::I32, s, ..) => {
   191	            let s = s.replace("_", "");
   192	            i32::from_str_by_radix(&s).expect("Parsing guarantees this works.").into()
   193	        }
   194	        LiteralVariant::Integer(IntegerType::I64, s, ..) => {
   195	            let s = s.replace("_", "");
   196	            i64::from_str_by_radix(&s).expect("Parsing guarantees this works.").into()
   197	        }
   198	        LiteralVariant::Integer(IntegerType::I128, s, ..) => {
   199	            let s = s.replace("_", "");
   200	            i128::from_str_by_radix(&s).expect("Parsing guarantees this works.").into()
   201	        }
   202	        LiteralVariant::None => halt_no_span2!(""),
   203	        LiteralVariant::Scalar(s) => {
   204	            SvmLiteralParam::Scalar(prepare_snarkvm_string(s, "scalar").parse().expect_tc(literal.span)?).into()
   205	        }
   206	        LiteralVariant::Signature(s) => {
   207	            let signature: Signature = s.parse().expect_tc(literal.span)?;
   208	            signature.into()
   209	        }
   210	        LiteralVariant::String(s) => Value::make_string(s.clone()),
   211	        LiteralVariant::Unsuffixed(s) => {
   212	            let unsuffixed = Value { id: None, contents: ValueVariants::Unsuffixed(s.clone()) };
   213	            unsuffixed.resolve_if_unsuffixed(expected_ty, literal.span)?
   214	        }
   215	    })
   216	}
   217	
   218	/// Resolves an unsuffixed operand for a unary operation by inferring its type based on the operation and an optional
   219	/// expected type. Uses predefined types (`Field` or `Group`) for specific operations, otherwise defaults to the expected
   220	/// type if available. Returns the resolved `Value` or an error if type resolution fails.
   221	fn resolve_unsuffixed_unary_op_operand(
   222	    val: &Value,
   223	    op: &UnaryOperation,
   224	    expected_ty: &Option<Type>,
   225	    span: &Span,
   226	) -> Result<Value> {
   227	    match op {
   228	        UnaryOperation::Inverse | UnaryOperation::Square | UnaryOperation::SquareRoot => {
   229	            // These ops only take a `field` and return a `field`
   230	            val.resolve_if_unsuffixed(&Some(Type::Field), *span)
   231	        }
   232	        UnaryOperation::ToXCoordinate | UnaryOperation::ToYCoordinate => {
   233	            // These ops only take a `Group`
   234	            val.resolve_if_unsuffixed(&Some(Type::Group), *span)
   235	        }
   236	        _ => {
   237	            // All other unary ops take the same type as the their return type
   238	            val.resolve_if_unsuffixed(expected_ty, *span)
   239	        }
   240	    }
   241	}
   242	
   243	/// Evaluate a unary operation.
   244	pub fn evaluate_unary(span: Span, op: UnaryOperation, value: &Value, expected_ty: &Option<Type>) -> Result<Value> {
   245	    let value = resolve_unsuffixed_unary_op_operand(value, &op, expected_ty, &span)?;
   246	    let ValueVariants::Svm(SvmValueParam::Plaintext(Plaintext::Literal(literal, ..))) = &value.contents else {
   247	        halt2!(span, "Type error");
   248	    };
   249	    let value_result: Value = match op {
   250	        UnaryOperation::Abs => match literal {
   251	            SvmLiteralParam::I8(x) => {
   252	                x.checked_abs().ok_or_else::<ConstEvalError, _>(|| fail2!(span, "abs overflow"))?.into()
   253	            }
   254	            SvmLiteralParam::I16(x) => {
   255	                x.checked_abs().ok_or_else::<ConstEvalError, _>(|| fail2!(span, "abs overlfow"))?.into()
   256	            }
   257	            SvmLiteralParam::I32(x) => {
   258	                x.checked_abs().ok_or_else::<ConstEvalError, _>(|| fail2!(span, "abs overlfow"))?.into()
   259	            }
   260	            SvmLiteralParam::I64(x) => {
   261	                x.checked_abs().ok_or_else::<ConstEvalError, _>(|| fail2!(span, "abs overlfow"))?.into()
   262	            }
   263	            SvmLiteralParam::I128(x) => {
   264	                x.checked_abs().ok_or_else::<ConstEvalError, _>(|| fail2!(span, "abs overlfow"))?.into()
   265	            }
   266	            _ => halt2!(span, "Type error"),
   267	        },
   268	        UnaryOperation::AbsWrapped => match literal {
   269	            SvmLiteralParam::I8(x) => (x.unsigned_abs() as i8).into(),
   270	            SvmLiteralParam::I16(x) => (x.unsigned_abs() as i16).into(),
   271	            SvmLiteralParam::I32(x) => (x.unsigned_abs() as i32).into(),
   272	            SvmLiteralParam::I64(x) => (x.unsigned_abs() as i64).into(),
   273	            SvmLiteralParam::I128(x) => (x.unsigned_abs() as i128).into(),
   274	            _ => halt2!(span, "Type error"),
   275	        },
   276	        UnaryOperation::Double => match literal {
   277	            SvmLiteralParam::Field(x) => <Field as Double>::double(x).into(),
   278	            SvmLiteralParam::Group(x) => <Group as Double>::double(x).into(),
   279	            _ => halt2!(span, "Type error"),
   280	        },
   281	        UnaryOperation::Inverse => match literal {
   282	            SvmLiteralParam::Field(x) => {
   283	                let Ok(y) = x.inverse() else {
   284	                    halt2!(span, "attempt to invert 0field");
   285	                };
   286	                y.into()
   287	            }
   288	            _ => halt2!(span, "Can only invert fields"),
   289	        },
   290	        UnaryOperation::Negate => match literal {
   291	            SvmLiteralParam::I8(x) => {
   292	                x.checked_neg().ok_or_else::<ConstEvalError, _>(|| fail2!(span, "negation overflow"))?.into()
   293	            }
   294	            SvmLiteralParam::I16(x) => {
   295	                x.checked_neg().ok_or_else::<ConstEvalError, _>(|| fail2!(span, "negation overflow"))?.into()
   296	            }
   297	            SvmLiteralParam::I32(x) => {
   298	                x.checked_neg().ok_or_else::<ConstEvalError, _>(|| fail2!(span, "negation overflow"))?.into()
   299	            }
   300	            SvmLiteralParam::I64(x) => {
   301	                x.checked_neg().ok_or_else::<ConstEvalError, _>(|| fail2!(span, "negation overflow"))?.into()
   302	            }
   303	            SvmLiteralParam::I128(x) => {
   304	                x.checked_neg().ok_or_else::<ConstEvalError, _>(|| fail2!(span, "negation overflow"))?.into()
   305	            }
   306	            SvmLiteralParam::Group(x) => (-*x).into(),
   307	            SvmLiteralParam::Field(x) => (-*x).into(),
   308	            _ => halt2!(span, "Type error"),
   309	        },
   310	        UnaryOperation::Not => match literal {
   311	            SvmLiteralParam::Boolean(x) => (!**x).into(),
   312	            SvmLiteralParam::U8(x) => (!**x).into(),
   313	            SvmLiteralParam::U16(x) => (!**x).into(),
   314	            SvmLiteralParam::U32(x) => (!**x).into(),
   315	            SvmLiteralParam::U64(x) => (!**x).into(),
   316	            SvmLiteralParam::U128(x) => (!**x).into(),
   317	            SvmLiteralParam::I8(x) => (!**x).into(),
   318	            SvmLiteralParam::I16(x) => (!**x).into(),
   319	            SvmLiteralParam::I32(x) => (!**x).into(),
   320	            SvmLiteralParam::I64(x) => (!**x).into(),
   321	            SvmLiteralParam::I128(x) => (!**x).into(),
   322	            _ => halt2!(span, "Type error"),
   323	        },
   324	        UnaryOperation::Square => match literal {
   325	            SvmLiteralParam::Field(x) => x.square().into(),
   326	            _ => halt2!(span, "Can only square fields"),
   327	        },
   328	        UnaryOperation::SquareRoot => match literal {
   329	            SvmLiteralParam::Field(x) => {
   330	                x.square_root().map_err::<ConstEvalError, _>(|e| fail2!(span, "square root failure: {e}"))?.into()
   331	            }
   332	            _ => halt2!(span, "Can only apply square_root to fields"),
   333	        },
   334	        UnaryOperation::ToXCoordinate => match literal {
   335	            SvmLiteral::Group(x) => x.to_x_coordinate().into(),
   336	            _ => tc_fail2!(),
   337	        },
   338	        UnaryOperation::ToYCoordinate => match literal {
   339	            SvmLiteral::Group(x) => x.to_y_coordinate().into(),
   340	            _ => tc_fail2!(),
   341	        },
   342	    };
   343	
   344	    Ok(value_result)
   345	}
   346

    17	use crate::CompilerState;
    18	
    19	use leo_ast::{Expression, Location, Node, NodeID, const_eval::Value};
    20	use leo_errors::StaticAnalyzerError;
    21	use leo_span::{Span, Symbol};

    23	use indexmap::IndexMap;
    24	
    25	/// Visitor that propagates constant values through the program.
    26	pub struct SsaConstPropagationVisitor<'a> {
    27	    pub state: &'a mut CompilerState,
    28	    /// Current program being analyzed.
    29	    pub program: Symbol,
    30	    /// Maps variable names to their constant values.
    31	    /// Only variables assigned constant values are tracked here.
    32	    pub constants: IndexMap<Symbol, Value>,
    33	    /// Have we actually modified the program at all?
    34	    pub changed: bool,
    35	}
    36	
    37	impl SsaConstPropagationVisitor<'_> {
    38	    /// Emit a `StaticAnalyzerError`.
    39	    pub fn emit_err(&self, err: StaticAnalyzerError) {
    40	        self.state.handler.emit_err(err);
    41	    }
    42	
    43	    /// Convert a Value to an Expression.
    44	    /// Returns the new expression and its node ID.
    45	    /// If the original node doesn't have a type, this will return None.
    46	    pub fn value_to_expression(&mut self, value: &Value, span: Span, id: NodeID) -> Option<(Expression, NodeID)> {
    47	        let ty = self.state.type_table.get(&id)?.clone();
    48	        let symbol_table = &self.state.symbol_table;
    49	        let struct_lookup = |loc: &Location| {
    50	            symbol_table
    51	                .lookup_struct(self.program, loc)
    52	                .unwrap()
    53	                .members
    54	                .iter()
    55	                .map(|mem| (mem.identifier.name, mem.type_.clone()))
    56	                .collect()
    57	        };
    58	        let new_expr = value.to_expression(span, &self.state.node_builder, &ty, &struct_lookup)?;
    59	        let new_id = new_expr.id();
    60	
    61	        // Copy the type information to the new node ID.
    62	        self.copy_types_recursively(&new_expr, &ty);
    63	
    64	        Some((new_expr, new_id))
    65	    }
    66	
    67	    /// Copy types for nested expressions based on the type structure.
    68	    /// This ensures that ALL expressions in the tree have proper type information.
    69	    fn copy_types_recursively(&mut self, expr: &Expression, ty: &leo_ast::Type) {
    70	        use leo_ast::Type;
    71	
    72	        self.state.type_table.insert(expr.id(), ty.clone());
    73	
    74	        // Then recursively handle nested expressions
    75	        match (expr, ty) {
    76	            (Expression::Array(array_expr), Type::Array(array_ty)) => {
    77	                for element in &array_expr.elements {
    78	                    self.copy_types_recursively(element, array_ty.element_type());
    79	                }
    80	            }
    81	            (Expression::Tuple(tuple_expr), Type::Tuple(tuple_ty)) => {
    82	                for (element, elem_ty) in tuple_expr.elements.iter().zip(tuple_ty.elements()) {
    83	                    self.copy_types_recursively(element, elem_ty);
    84	                }
    85	            }
    86	            (Expression::Composite(composite_expr), Type::Composite(composite_ty)) => {
    87	                // We only look for structs here (not records) because `copy_types_recursively` is
    88	                // only called from `value_to_expression`, which never produces record expressions.
    89	                let member_types: Vec<leo_ast::Type> = self
    90	                    .state
    91	                    .symbol_table
    92	                    .lookup_struct(self.program, composite_ty.path.expect_global_location())
    93	                    .map(|struct_def| struct_def.members.iter().map(|m| m.type_.clone()).collect())
    94	                    .unwrap_or_default();
    95	                for (member, member_ty) in composite_expr.members.iter().zip(member_types.iter()) {
    96	                    if let Some(expr) = &member.expression {
    97	                        self.copy_types_recursively(expr, member_ty);
    98	                    }
    99	                }
   100	            }
   101	            _ => {
   102	                // For leaf expressions (literals, etc.), we've already set the type above
   103	            }
   104	        }
   105	    }
   106	}
   107

    17	use super::SsaConstPropagationVisitor;
    18	
    19	use leo_ast::{
    20	    const_eval::{self, Value},
    21	    *,
    22	};
    23	use leo_errors::StaticAnalyzerError;
    24	
    25	const VALUE_ERROR: &str = "A non-future value should always be able to be converted into an expression";
    26	
    27	impl AstReconstructor for SsaConstPropagationVisitor<'_> {
    28	    type AdditionalInput = ();
    29	    type AdditionalOutput = Option<Value>;
    30	
    31	    /// Reconstruct a path expression. If the path refers to a variable that has
    32	    /// a constant value, replace it with that constant.
    33	    fn reconstruct_path(&mut self, input: Path, _additional: &()) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
    34	        // In SSA form, paths should refer to local variables (or composite members).
    35	        // Check if this variable has a constant value.
    36	        let identifier_name = input.identifier().name;
    37	
    38	        if let Some(constant_value) = self.constants.get(&identifier_name).cloned() {
    39	            // Replace the path with the constant value.
    40	            let span = input.span();
    41	            let id = input.id();
    42	            let (new_expr, _) = self.value_to_expression(&constant_value, span, id).expect(VALUE_ERROR);
    43	            self.changed = true;
    44	            (new_expr, Some(constant_value))
    45	        } else {
    46	            // No constant value for this variable, keep the path as is.
    47	            (input.into(), None)
    48	        }
    49	    }
    50	
    51	    /// Reconstruct a literal expression and convert it to a Value.
    52	    fn reconstruct_literal(&mut self, mut input: Literal, _additional: &()) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
    53	        let type_info = self.state.type_table.get(&input.id());
    54	
    55	        // If this is an optional, then unwrap it first.
    56	        let type_info = type_info.as_ref().map(|ty| match ty {
    57	            Type::Optional(opt) => *opt.inner.clone(),
    58	            _ => ty.clone(),
    59	        });
    60	
    61	        if let Ok(value) = const_eval::literal_to_value(&input, &type_info) {
    62	            match input.variant {
    63	                LiteralVariant::Address(ref s) if s.ends_with("aleo") => {
    64	                    // Do not fold program names as the VM needs to handle them directly
    65	                    (input.into(), None)
    66	                }
    67	
    68	                // If we know the type of an unsuffixed literal, might as well change it to a suffixed literal.
    69	                LiteralVariant::Unsuffixed(s) => {
    70	                    match type_info.expect("Expected type information to be available") {
    71	                        Type::Integer(ty) => input.variant = LiteralVariant::Integer(ty, s),
    72	                        Type::Field => input.variant = LiteralVariant::Field(s),
    73	                        Type::Group => input.variant = LiteralVariant::Group(s),
    74	                        Type::Scalar => input.variant = LiteralVariant::Scalar(s),
    75	                        _ => panic!("Type checking should have prevented this."),
    76	                    }
    77	                    (input.into(), Some(value))
    78	                }
    79	                _ => (input.into(), Some(value)),
    80	            }
    81	        } else {
    82	            (input.into(), None)
    83	        }
    84	    }
    85	
    86	    /// Reconstruct a binary expression and fold it if both operands are constants.
    87	    fn reconstruct_binary(
    88	        &mut self,
    89	        input: BinaryExpression,
    90	        _additional: &(),
    91	    ) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
    92	        let span = input.span();
    93	        let input_id = input.id();
    94	
    95	        let (left, lhs_opt_value) = self.reconstruct_expression(input.left, &());
    96	        let (right, rhs_opt_value) = self.reconstruct_expression(input.right, &());
    97	
    98	        if let (Some(lhs_value), Some(rhs_value)) = (lhs_opt_value, rhs_opt_value) {
    99	            // We were able to evaluate both operands, so we can evaluate this expression.
   100	            match const_eval::evaluate_binary(
   101	                span,
   102	                input.op,
   103	                &lhs_value,
   104	                &rhs_value,
   105	                &self.state.type_table.get(&input_id),
   106	            ) {
   107	                Ok(new_value) => {
   108	                    let (new_expr, _) = self.value_to_expression(&new_value, span, input_id).expect(VALUE_ERROR);
   109	                    self.changed = true;
   110	                    return (new_expr, Some(new_value));
   111	                }
   112	                Err(err) => self
   113	                    .emit_err(StaticAnalyzerError::compile_time_binary_op(lhs_value, rhs_value, input.op, err, span)),
   114	            }
   115	        }
   116	
   117	        (BinaryExpression { left, right, ..input }.into(), None)
   118	    }
   119	
   120	    /// Reconstruct a unary expression and fold it if the operand is a constant.
   121	    fn reconstruct_unary(&mut self, input: UnaryExpression, _additional: &()) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
   122	        let input_id = input.id();
   123	        let span = input.span;
   124	        let (receiver, opt_value) = self.reconstruct_expression(input.receiver, &());
   125	
   126	        if let Some(value) = opt_value {
   127	            // We were able to evaluate the operand, so we can evaluate the expression.
   128	            match const_eval::evaluate_unary(span, input.op, &value, &self.state.type_table.get(&input_id)) {
   129	                Ok(new_value) => {
   130	                    let (new_expr, _) = self.value_to_expression(&new_value, span, input_id).expect(VALUE_ERROR);
   131	                    self.changed = true;
   132	                    return (new_expr, Some(new_value));
   133	                }
   134	                Err(err) => self.emit_err(StaticAnalyzerError::compile_time_unary_op(value, input.op, err, span)),
   135	            }
   136	        }
   137	        (UnaryExpression { receiver, ..input }.into(), None)
   138	    }
   139	
   140	    /// Reconstruct a ternary expression and fold it if the condition is a constant.
   141	    fn reconstruct_ternary(
   142	        &mut self,
   143	        input: TernaryExpression,
   144	        _additional: &(),
   145	    ) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
   146	        let (cond, cond_value) = self.reconstruct_expression(input.condition, &());
   147	
   148	        match cond_value.and_then(|v| v.try_into().ok()) {
   149	            Some(true) => {
   150	                self.changed = true;
   151	                self.reconstruct_expression(input.if_true, &())
   152	            }
   153	            Some(false) => {
   154	                self.changed = true;
   155	                self.reconstruct_expression(input.if_false, &())
   156	            }
   157	            _ => (
   158	                TernaryExpression {
   159	                    condition: cond,
   160	                    if_true: self.reconstruct_expression(input.if_true, &()).0,
   161	                    if_false: self.reconstruct_expression(input.if_false, &()).0,
   162	                    ..input
   163	                }
   164	                .into(),
   165	                None,
   166	            ),
   167	        }
   168	    }
   169	
   170	    /// Reconstruct an array access expression and fold it if array and index are constants.
   171	    fn reconstruct_array_access(
   172	        &mut self,
   173	        input: ArrayAccess,
   174	        _additional: &(),
   175	    ) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
   176	        let span = input.span();
   177	        let id = input.id();
   178	
   179	        let (array, array_opt) = self.reconstruct_expression(input.array, &());
   180	        let (index, index_opt) = self.reconstruct_expression(input.index, &());
   181	
   182	        if let Some(index_value) = index_opt
   183	            && let Some(array_value) = array_opt
   184	        {
   185	            let result_value =
   186	                array_value.array_index(index_value.as_u32().unwrap() as usize).expect("We already checked bounds.");
   187	            self.changed = true;
   188	            let (new_expr, _) = self.value_to_expression(&result_value, span, id).expect(VALUE_ERROR);
   189	            return (new_expr, Some(result_value.clone()));
   190	        }
   191	
   192	        (ArrayAccess { array, index, ..input }.into(), None)
   193	    }
   194	
   195	    /// Reconstruct an array expression and fold it if all elements are constants.
   196	    fn reconstruct_array(
   197	        &mut self,
   198	        mut input: ArrayExpression,
   199	        _additional: &(),
   200	    ) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
   201	        let mut values = Vec::new();
   202	        let mut elements_changed = false;
   203	        input.elements.iter_mut().for_each(|element| {
   204	            let old_element = element.clone();
   205	            let (new_element, value_opt) = self.reconstruct_expression(std::mem::take(element), &());
   206	            // Check if the element actually changed (not just its structure, but if it's a different expression)
   207	            if old_element.id() != new_element.id() {
   208	                elements_changed = true;
   209	            }
   210	            if let Some(value) = value_opt {
   211	                values.push(value);
   212	            }
   213	            *element = new_element;
   214	        });
   215	        // Only set changed if elements actually changed. Don't set changed just because
   216	        // we can evaluate the array - that would cause an infinite loop since the array
   217	        // expression structure doesn't change.
   218	        if elements_changed {
   219	            self.changed = true;
   220	        }
   221	
   222	        if values.len() == input.elements.len() {
   223	            (input.into(), Some(Value::make_array(values.into_iter())))
   224	        } else {
   225	            (input.into(), None)
   226	        }
   227	    }
   228	
   229	    /// Reconstruct a tuple expression and fold it if all elements are constants.
   230	    fn reconstruct_tuple(
   231	        &mut self,
   232	        mut input: TupleExpression,
   233	        _additional: &(),
   234	    ) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
   235	        let mut values = Vec::with_capacity(input.elements.len());
   236	        let mut elements_changed = false;
   237	        for expr in input.elements.iter_mut() {
   238	            let old_expr = expr.clone();
   239	            let (new_expr, opt_value) = self.reconstruct_expression(std::mem::take(expr), &());
   240	            // Check if the element actually changed
   241	            if old_expr.id() != new_expr.id() {
   242	                elements_changed = true;
   243	            }
   244	            *expr = new_expr;
   245	            if let Some(value) = opt_value {
   246	                values.push(value);
   247	            }
   248	        }
   249	
   250	        // Only set changed if elements actually changed. Don't set changed just because
   251	        // we can evaluate the tuple - that would cause an infinite loop since the tuple
   252	        // expression structure doesn't change.
   253	        if elements_changed {
   254	            self.changed = true;
   255	        }
   256	
   257	        let opt_value = if values.len() == input.elements.len() { Some(Value::make_tuple(values)) } else { None };
   258	
   259	        (input.into(), opt_value)
   260	    }
   261	
   262	    /* Statements */
   263	    /// Reconstruct a definition statement. If the RHS evaluates to a constant, track it
   264	    /// in the constants map for propagation.
   265	    fn reconstruct_definition(&mut self, mut input: DefinitionStatement) -> (Statement, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
   266	        // Reconstruct the RHS expression first.
   267	        let (new_value, opt_value) = self.reconstruct_expression(input.value, &());
   268	
   269	        if let Some(value) = opt_value {
   270	            match &input.place {
   271	                DefinitionPlace::Single(identifier) => {
   272	                    self.constants.insert(identifier.name, value);
   273	                }
   274	                DefinitionPlace::Multiple(identifiers) => {
   275	                    for (i, id) in identifiers.iter().enumerate() {
   276	                        if let Some(v) = value.tuple_index(i) {
   277	                            self.constants.insert(id.name, v);
   278	                        }
   279	                    }
   280	                }
   281	            }
   282	        }
   283	
   284	        input.value = new_value;
   285	
   286	        (input.into(), None)
   287	    }
   288	
   289	    fn reconstruct_assign(&mut self, _input: AssignStatement) -> (Statement, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
   290	        panic!("there should be no assignments at this stage");
   291	    }
   292	}

   107	        containing_function: Location, // The function that contains the async block.
   108	        block: crate::NodeID,
   109	        names: BTreeMap<Vec<Symbol>, Value>, // Use a `BTreeMap` here because `HashMap` does not implement `Hash`.
   110	    },
   111	}
   112	
   113	impl fmt::Display for AsyncExecution {
   114	    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {
   115	        write!(f, " async call to ")?;
   116	
   117	        match self {
   118	            AsyncExecution::AsyncFunctionCall { function, .. } => {
   119	                write!(f, "{function}")
   120	            }
   121	            AsyncExecution::AsyncBlock { containing_function, .. } => {
   122	                write!(f, "{containing_function}/<async block>")
   123	            }
   124	        }
   125	    }
   126	}
   127	
   128	fn hash_plaintext<H>(pt: &SvmPlaintext, state: &mut H)
   129	where
   130	    H: Hasher,
   131	{
   132	    match pt {
   133	        Plaintext::Literal(literal, ..) => {
   134	            6u8.hash(state);
   135	            literal.hash(state);
   136	        }
   137	        Plaintext::Struct(index_map, ..) => {
   138	            7u8.hash(state);
   139	            index_map.len().hash(state);
   140	            // The correctness of this hash depends on the members being
   141	            // in the same order for each type.
   142	            index_map.iter().for_each(|(key, value)| {
   143	                key.hash(state);
   144	                hash_plaintext(value, state);
   145	            });
   146	        }
   147	        Plaintext::Array(vec, ..) => {
   148	            8u8.hash(state);
   149	            vec.len().hash(state);
   150	            vec.iter().for_each(|pt0| hash_plaintext(pt0, state));
   151	        }
   152	    }
   153	}
   154	
   155	impl Hash for ValueVariants {
   156	    fn hash<H>(&self, state: &mut H)
   157	    where
   158	        H: Hasher,
   159	    {
   160	        use ValueVariants::*;
   161	
   162	        match self {
   163	            Unit => 0u8.hash(state),
   164	            Tuple(vec) => {
   165	                1u8.hash(state);
   166	                vec.len().hash(state);
   167	            }
   168	            Unsuffixed(s) => {
   169	                2u8.hash(state);
   170	                s.hash(state);
   171	            }
   172	            Future(async_executions) => {
   173	                3u8.hash(state);
   174	                async_executions.hash(state);
   175	            }
   176	            Svm(value) => match value {
   177	                SvmValueParam::Record(record) => {
   178	                    4u8.hash(state);
   179	                    (**record.version()).hash(state);
   180	                    record.nonce().hash(state);
   181	                    // NOTE - we don't actually hash the data or owner. Thus this is
   182	                    // a terrible hash function with many collisions.
   183	                    // This shouldn't matter as the only place where we hash this is in
   184	                    // keys for mappings, which cannot be records.
   185	                }
   186	                SvmValueParam::Future(future) => {
   187	                    5u8.hash(state);
   188	                    future.program_id().hash(state);
   189	                    future.function_name().hash(state);
   190	                    // Ditto - we don't hash the arguments.
   191	                }
   192	                SvmValueParam::Plaintext(plaintext) => {
   193	                    hash_plaintext(plaintext, state);
   194	                }
   195	                SvmValueParam::DynamicRecord(record) => {
   196	                    6u8.hash(state);
   197	                    (**record.version()).hash(state);
   198	                    record.nonce().hash(state);
   199	                }
   200	                SvmValueParam::DynamicFuture(future) => {
   201	                    7u8.hash(state);
   202	                    future.program_name().hash(state);
   203	                    future.function_name().hash(state);
   204	                }
   205	            },
   206	            String(s) => {
   207	                9u8.hash(state);
   208	                s.hash(state);
   209	            }
   210	        }
   211	    }
   212	}
   213	
   214	impl From<ValueVariants> for Value {
   215	    fn from(contents: ValueVariants) -> Self {
   216	        Value { id: None, contents }
   217	    }

   229	        $(

   239	                    ).into()
   240	                }
   241	            }

   244	                fn from(x: snarkvm::prelude::$variant<CurrentNetwork>) -> Self {
   245	                    ValueVariants::Svm(SvmValueParam::Plaintext(
   246	                        Plaintext::Literal(

   255	                type Error = ();

   259	                        ValueVariants::Svm(SvmValueParam::Plaintext(Plaintext::Literal(SvmLiteralParam::$variant(x), _))) => Ok(*x),

   269	                        _ => None,

   271	                }
   272	            }

   274	    };

   410	impl fmt::Display for Value {
   411	    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {
   412	        match &self.contents {
   413	            ValueVariants::Unit => "()".fmt(f),
   414	            ValueVariants::Svm(SvmValueParam::Plaintext(Plaintext::Struct(struct_, ..))) => {
   415	                if let Some(id) = &self.id {
   416	                    write!(f, "{id} ")?
   417	                }
   418	                let mut debug_map = f.debug_map();
   419	                for (key, value) in struct_ {
   420	                    debug_map.entry(key, value);
   421	                }
   422	                debug_map.finish()
   423	            }
   424	            ValueVariants::Svm(value) => value.fmt(f),
   425	            ValueVariants::Tuple(vec) => write!(f, "({})", vec.iter().format(", ")),
   426	            ValueVariants::Unsuffixed(s) => s.fmt(f),
   427	            ValueVariants::Future(_async_executions) => "Future".fmt(f),
   428	            ValueVariants::String(s) => write!(f, "\"{s}\""),
   429	        }
   430	    }
   431	}

   433	impl Value {
   434	    pub fn lt(&self, rhs: &Self) -> Option<bool> {
   435	        use SvmLiteralParam::*;
   436	
   437	        let literal0: &SvmLiteral = self.try_as_ref()?;
   438	        let literal1: &SvmLiteral = rhs.try_as_ref()?;
   439	
   440	        let value = match (literal0, literal1) {
   441	            (I8(val0), I8(val1)) => val0 < val1,
   442	            (I16(val0), I16(val1)) => val0 < val1,
   443	            (I32(val0), I32(val1)) => val0 < val1,
   444	            (I64(val0), I64(val1)) => val0 < val1,
   445	            (I128(val0), I128(val1)) => val0 < val1,
   446	            (U8(val0), U8(val1)) => val0 < val1,
   447	            (U16(val0), U16(val1)) => val0 < val1,
   448	            (U32(val0), U32(val1)) => val0 < val1,
   449	            (U64(val0), U64(val1)) => val0 < val1,
   450	            (U128(val0), U128(val1)) => val0 < val1,
   451	            (Field(val0), Field(val1)) => val0 < val1,
   452	            _ => return None,
   453	        };
   454	
   455	        Some(value)
   456	    }
   457	
   458	    pub fn lte(&self, rhs: &Self) -> Option<bool> {
   459	        use SvmLiteralParam::*;
   460	
   461	        let literal0: &SvmLiteral = self.try_as_ref()?;
   462	        let literal1: &SvmLiteral = rhs.try_as_ref()?;
   463	
   464	        let value = match (literal0, literal1) {
   465	            (I8(val0), I8(val1)) => val0 <= val1,
   466	            (I16(val0), I16(val1)) => val0 <= val1,
   467	            (I32(val0), I32(val1)) => val0 <= val1,
   468	            (I64(val0), I64(val1)) => val0 <= val1,
   469	            (I128(val0), I128(val1)) => val0 <= val1,
   470	            (U8(val0), U8(val1)) => val0 <= val1,
   471	            (U16(val0), U16(val1)) => val0 <= val1,
   472	            (U32(val0), U32(val1)) => val0 <= val1,
   473	            (U64(val0), U64(val1)) => val0 <= val1,
   474	            (U128(val0), U128(val1)) => val0 <= val1,
   475	            (Field(val0), Field(val1)) => val0 <= val1,
   476	            _ => return None,
   477	        };
   478	
   479	        Some(value)
   480	    }
   481	
   482	    pub fn gt(&self, rhs: &Self) -> Option<bool> {
   483	        rhs.lt(self)
   484	    }
   485	
   486	    pub fn gte(&self, rhs: &Self) -> Option<bool> {
   487	        rhs.lte(self)
   488	    }
   489

   499	            SvmLiteralParam::I8(x) => x.wrapping_add(1).into(),

   848	    pub fn to_expression(
   849	        &self,
   850	        span: Span,
   851	        node_builder: &NodeBuilder,
   852	        ty: &Type,
   853	        struct_lookup: &dyn Fn(&Location) -> Vec<(Symbol, Type)>,
   854	    ) -> Option<Expression> {
   855	        use crate::{Literal, TupleExpression, UnitExpression};
   856	
   857	        let id = node_builder.next_id();
   858	        let expression = match &self.contents {
   859	            ValueVariants::Unit => UnitExpression { span, id }.into(),
   860	            ValueVariants::Tuple(vec) => {
   861	                let Type::Tuple(tuple_type) = ty else {
   862	                    return None;
   863	                };
   864	
   865	                if vec.len() != tuple_type.elements().len() {
   866	                    return None;
   867	                }
   868	
   869	                TupleExpression {
   870	                    span,
   871	                    id,
   872	                    elements: vec
   873	                        .iter()
   874	                        .zip(tuple_type.elements())
   875	                        .map(|(val, ty)| val.to_expression(span, node_builder, ty, struct_lookup))
   876	                        .collect::<Option<Vec<_>>>()?,
   877	                }
   878	                .into()
   879	            }
   880	            ValueVariants::Unsuffixed(s) => Literal::unsuffixed(s.clone(), span, id).into(),
   881	            ValueVariants::Svm(value) => match value {
   882	                SvmValueParam::Plaintext(plaintext) => {
   883	                    plaintext_to_expression(plaintext, span, node_builder, ty, &struct_lookup)?
   884	                }
   885	                SvmValueParam::Record(..) => return None,
   886	                SvmValueParam::Future(..) => return None,
   887	                SvmValueParam::DynamicRecord(..) => return None,
   888	                SvmValueParam::DynamicFuture(..) => return None,
   889	            },
   890	            ValueVariants::Future(..) => return None,
   891	            ValueVariants::String(value) => Literal::string(value.clone(), span, id).into(),
   892	        };
   893	
   894	        Some(expression)
   895	    }
   896	}
   897	
   898	#[allow(clippy::type_complexity)]
   899	fn plaintext_to_expression(
   900	    plaintext: &SvmPlaintext,
   901	    span: Span,
   902	    node_builder: &NodeBuilder,
   903	    ty: &Type,
   904	    struct_lookup: &dyn Fn(&Location) -> Vec<(Symbol, Type)>,
   905	) -> Option<Expression> {
   906	    use crate::{ArrayExpression, CompositeExpression, CompositeFieldInitializer, Identifier, IntegerType, Literal};
   907	
   908	    let id = node_builder.next_id();
   909	
   910	    let expression = match plaintext {
   911	        Plaintext::Literal(literal, ..) => match literal {
   912	            SvmLiteralParam::Address(address) => {
   913	                Literal::address(address.to_string(), span, node_builder.next_id()).into()
   914	            }
   915	            SvmLiteralParam::Boolean(boolean) => Literal::boolean(**boolean, span, node_builder.next_id()).into(),
   916	            SvmLiteralParam::Field(field) => {
   917	                let mut s = field.to_string();
   918	                // Strip off the `field` suffix.
   919	                s.truncate(s.len() - 5);
   920	                Literal::field(s, span, id).into()
   921	            }
   922	            SvmLiteralParam::Group(group) => {
   923	                let mut s = group.to_string();
   924	                // Strip off the `group` suffix.
   925	                s.truncate(s.len() - 5);
   926	                Literal::group(s, span, id).into()
   927	            }
   928	            SvmLiteralParam::I8(int) => Literal::integer(IntegerType::I8, (**int).to_string(), span, id).into(),
   929	            SvmLiteralParam::I16(int) => Literal::integer(IntegerType::I16, (**int).to_string(), span, id).into(),
   930	            SvmLiteralParam::I32(int) => Literal::integer(IntegerType::I32, (**int).to_string(), span, id).into(),
   931	            SvmLiteralParam::I64(int) => Literal::integer(IntegerType::I64, (**int).to_string(), span, id).into(),
   932	            SvmLiteralParam::I128(int) => Literal::integer(IntegerType::I128, (**int).to_string(), span, id).into(),
   933	            SvmLiteralParam::U8(int) => Literal::integer(IntegerType::U8, (**int).to_string(), span, id).into(),
   934	            SvmLiteralParam::U16(int) => Literal::integer(IntegerType::U16, (**int).to_string(), span, id).into(),
   935	            SvmLiteralParam::U32(int) => Literal::integer(IntegerType::U32, (**int).to_string(), span, id).into(),
   936	            SvmLiteralParam::U64(int) => Literal::integer(IntegerType::U64, (**int).to_string(), span, id).into(),
   937	            SvmLiteralParam::U128(int) => Literal::integer(IntegerType::U128, (**int).to_string(), span, id).into(),
   938	            SvmLiteralParam::Scalar(scalar) => {
   939	                let mut s = scalar.to_string();
   940	                // Strip off the `scalar` suffix.
   941	                s.truncate(s.len() - 6);
   942	                Literal::scalar(s, span, id).into()
   943	            }
   944	            SvmLiteralParam::Signature(signature) => {
   945	                Literal::address(signature.to_string(), span, node_builder.next_id()).into()
   946	            }
   947	            SvmLiteralParam::String(..) => return None,
   948	            SvmLiteralParam::Identifier(id) => {
   949	                // id.to_string() returns `'name'`; strip the surrounding single quotes.
   950	                let s = id.to_string();
   951	                let name = s.trim_matches('\'').to_string();
   952	                Literal::identifier(name, span, node_builder.next_id()).into()
   953	            }
   954	        },
   955	        Plaintext::Struct(index_map, ..) => {
   956	            let Type::Composite(composite_type) = ty else {
   957	                return None;
   958	            };
   959	            let composite_location = &composite_type.path.expect_global_location();
   960	            let iter_members = struct_lookup(composite_location);
   961	            CompositeExpression {
   962	                span,
   963	                id,
   964	                path: composite_type.path.clone(),
   965	                // If we were able to construct a Value, the const arguments must have already been resolved
   966	                // and inserted appropriately.
   967	                const_arguments: Vec::new(),
   968	                members: iter_members
   969	                    .into_iter()
   970	                    .map(|(sym, ty)| {
   971	                        let svm_identifier: snarkvm::prelude::Identifier<CurrentNetwork> =
   972	                            sym.to_string().parse().ok()?;
   973	                        Some(CompositeFieldInitializer {
   974	                            span,
   975	                            id: node_builder.next_id(),
   976	                            identifier: Identifier::new(sym, node_builder.next_id()),
   977	                            expression: Some(plaintext_to_expression(
   978	                                index_map.get(&svm_identifier)?,
   979	                                span,
   980	                                node_builder,
   981	                                &ty,
   982	                                &struct_lookup,
   983	                            )?),
   984	                        })
   985	                    })
   986	                    .collect::<Option<Vec<_>>>()?,
   987	            }
   988	            .into()
   989	        }
   990	        Plaintext::Array(vec, ..) => {
   991	            let Type::Array(array_ty) = ty else {
   992	                return None;
   993	            };
   994	            ArrayExpression {
   995	                span,
   996	                id,
   997	                elements: vec
   998	                    .iter()
   999	                    .map(|pt| plaintext_to_expression(pt, span, node_builder, &array_ty.element_type, &struct_lookup))
  1000	                    .collect::<Option<Vec<_>>>()?,
  1001	            }
  1002	            .into()
  1003	        }
  1004	    };
  1005	
  1006	    Some(expression)
  1007	}

    17	use leo_ast::{
    18	    const_eval::{self, Value},
    19	    *,
    20	};
    21	use leo_errors::StaticAnalyzerError;
    22	
    23	use super::ConstPropagationVisitor;
    24	
    25	const VALUE_ERROR: &str = "A non-future value should always be able to be converted into an expression";
    26	
    27	impl AstReconstructor for ConstPropagationVisitor<'_> {
    28	    type AdditionalInput = ();
    29	    type AdditionalOutput = Option<Value>;
    30	
    31	    /* Types */
    32	    fn reconstruct_array_type(&mut self, input: leo_ast::ArrayType) -> (leo_ast::Type, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
    33	        let (length, opt_value) = self.reconstruct_expression(*input.length, &());
    34	
    35	        // If we can't evaluate this array length, keep track of it for error reporting later
    36	        if opt_value.is_none() {
    37	            self.array_length_not_evaluated = Some(length.span());
    38	        }
    39	
    40	        (
    41	            leo_ast::Type::Array(leo_ast::ArrayType {
    42	                element_type: Box::new(self.reconstruct_type(*input.element_type).0),
    43	                length: Box::new(length),
    44	            }),
    45	            Default::default(),
    46	        )
    47	    }
    48	
    49	    /* Expressions */
    50	    fn reconstruct_expression(&mut self, input: Expression, _additional: &()) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
    51	        let opt_old_type = self.state.type_table.get(&input.id());
    52	        let (new_expr, opt_value) = match input {
    53	            Expression::Array(array) => self.reconstruct_array(array, &()),
    54	            Expression::ArrayAccess(access) => self.reconstruct_array_access(*access, &()),
    55	            Expression::Intrinsic(intr) => self.reconstruct_intrinsic(*intr, &()),
    56	            Expression::Async(async_) => self.reconstruct_async(async_, &()),
    57	            Expression::Binary(binary) => self.reconstruct_binary(*binary, &()),
    58	            Expression::Call(call) => self.reconstruct_call(*call, &()),
    59	            Expression::DynamicCall(dc) => self.reconstruct_dynamic_call(*dc, &()),
    60	            Expression::Cast(cast) => self.reconstruct_cast(*cast, &()),
    61	            Expression::Composite(composite) => self.reconstruct_composite_init(composite, &()),
    62	            Expression::Err(err) => self.reconstruct_err(err, &()),
    63	            Expression::Path(path) => self.reconstruct_path(path, &()),
    64	            Expression::Literal(value) => self.reconstruct_literal(value, &()),
    65	            Expression::MemberAccess(access) => self.reconstruct_member_access(*access, &()),
    66	            Expression::Repeat(repeat) => self.reconstruct_repeat(*repeat, &()),
    67	            Expression::Ternary(ternary) => self.reconstruct_ternary(*ternary, &()),
    68	            Expression::Tuple(tuple) => self.reconstruct_tuple(tuple, &()),
    69	            Expression::TupleAccess(access) => self.reconstruct_tuple_access(*access, &()),
    70	            Expression::Unary(unary) => self.reconstruct_unary(*unary, &()),
    71	            Expression::Unit(unit) => self.reconstruct_unit(unit, &()),
    72	        };
    73	
    74	        // If the expression was in the type table before, make an entry for the new expression.
    75	        if let Some(old_type) = opt_old_type {
    76	            self.state.type_table.insert(new_expr.id(), old_type);
    77	        }
    78	
    79	        (new_expr, opt_value)
    80	    }
    81	
    82	    fn reconstruct_composite_init(
    83	        &mut self,
    84	        mut input: CompositeExpression,
    85	        _additional: &(),
    86	    ) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
    87	        let mut values = Vec::new();
    88	        input.const_arguments.iter_mut().for_each(|arg| {
    89	            *arg = self.reconstruct_expression(std::mem::take(arg), &()).0;
    90	        });
    91	        for member in input.members.iter_mut() {
    92	            let expression =
    93	                member.expression.take().unwrap_or_else(|| Path::from(member.identifier).to_local().into());
    94	            let (new_expr, value_opt) = self.reconstruct_expression(expression, &());
    95	            member.expression = Some(new_expr);
    96	            if let Some(value) = value_opt {
    97	                values.push(value);
    98	            }
    99	        }
   100	
   101	        if values.len() == input.members.len() && input.const_arguments.is_empty() {
   102	            let value = Value::make_struct(
   103	                input.members.iter().map(|mem| mem.identifier.name).zip(values),
   104	                input.path.expect_global_location().clone(),
   105	            );
   106	            (input.into(), Some(value))
   107	        } else {
   108	            (input.into(), None)
   109	        }
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    fn reconstruct_ternary(
   113	        &mut self,
   114	        input: TernaryExpression,
   115	        _additional: &(),
   116	    ) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
   117	        let (cond, cond_value) = self.reconstruct_expression(input.condition, &());
   118	
   119	        match cond_value.and_then(|v| v.try_into().ok()) {
   120	            Some(true) => self.reconstruct_expression(input.if_true, &()),
   121	            Some(false) => self.reconstruct_expression(input.if_false, &()),
   122	            _ => (
   123	                TernaryExpression {
   124	                    condition: cond,
   125	                    if_true: self.reconstruct_expression(input.if_true, &()).0,
   126	                    if_false: self.reconstruct_expression(input.if_false, &()).0,
   127	                    ..input
   128	                }
   129	                .into(),
   130	                None,
   131	            ),
   132	        }
   133	    }
   134	
   135	    fn reconstruct_array_access(
   136	        &mut self,
   137	        input: ArrayAccess,
   138	        _additional: &(),
   139	    ) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
   140	        let span = input.span();
   141	        let id = input.id();
   142	        let array_id = input.array.id();
   143	        let (array, array_opt) = self.reconstruct_expression(input.array, &());
   144	        let (index, index_opt) = self.reconstruct_expression(input.index, &());
   145	        if let Some(index_value) = index_opt {
   146	            // We can perform compile time bounds checking.
   147	
   148	            let ty = self.state.type_table.get(&array_id);
   149	            let Some(Type::Array(array_ty)) = ty else {
   150	                panic!("Type checking guaranteed that this is an array.");
   151	            };
   152	            let len = array_ty.length.as_u32();
   153	
   154	            if let Some(len) = len {
   155	                let index_in_bounds = matches!(index_value.as_u32(), Some(index) if index < len);
   156	
   157	                if !index_in_bounds {
   158	                    // Only emit a bounds error if we have no other errors yet.
   159	                    // This prevents a chain of redundant error messages when a loop is unrolled.
   160	                    if !self.state.handler.had_errors() {
   161	                        // Get the integer string with no suffix.
   162	                        let integer_with_suffix = index_value.to_string();
   163	                        let suffix_index = integer_with_suffix.find(['i', 'u']).unwrap_or(integer_with_suffix.len());
   164	                        self.emit_err(StaticAnalyzerError::array_bounds(
   165	                            &integer_with_suffix[..suffix_index],
   166	                            len,
   167	                            span,
   168	                        ));
   169	                    }
   170	                } else if let Some(array_value) = array_opt {
   171	                    // We're in bounds and we can evaluate the array at compile time, so just return the value.
   172	                    let result_value = array_value
   173	                        .array_index(index_value.as_u32().unwrap() as usize)
   174	                        .expect("We already checked bounds.");
   175	                    return (
   176	                        self.value_to_expression(&result_value, span, id).expect(VALUE_ERROR),
   177	                        Some(result_value.clone()),
   178	                    );
   179	                }
   180	            }
   181	        } else {
   182	            self.array_index_not_evaluated = Some(index.span());
   183	        }
   184	        (ArrayAccess { array, index, ..input }.into(), None)
   185	    }
   186	
   187	    fn reconstruct_intrinsic(
   188	        &mut self,
   189	        mut input: leo_ast::IntrinsicExpression,
   190	        _additional: &(),
   191	    ) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
   192	        let mut values = Vec::new();
   193	        for argument in input.arguments.iter_mut() {
   194	            let (new_argument, opt_value) = self.reconstruct_expression(std::mem::take(argument), &());
   195	            *argument = new_argument;
   196	            if let Some(value) = opt_value {
   197	                values.push(value);
   198	            }
   199	        }
   200	
   201	        // Reconstruct type parameters, input types, and return types so that const identifiers
   202	        // inside array lengths are replaced with their evaluated values. This ensures, for
   203	        // example, `[u32; N]` where `const N: u32 = 5;` becomes `[u32; 5]`, and that unresolved
   204	        // lengths are reported via `array_length_not_evaluated` at the fixed point.
   205	        input.type_parameters =
   206	            input.type_parameters.into_iter().map(|(ty, span)| (self.reconstruct_type(ty).0, span)).collect();
   207	        input.input_types =
   208	            input.input_types.into_iter().map(|(mode, ty, span)| (mode, self.reconstruct_type(ty).0, span)).collect();
   209	        input.return_types =
   210	            input.return_types.into_iter().map(|(mode, ty, span)| (mode, self.reconstruct_type(ty).0, span)).collect();
   211	
   212	        let intrinsic = Intrinsic::from_symbol(input.name, &input.type_parameters)
   213	            .expect("Type checking guarantees this is valid.");
   214	
   215	        if values.len() == input.arguments.len() && intrinsic.is_pure() {
   216	            // We've evaluated every argument, and this function has no side
   217	            // effects, so maybe we can compute the result at compile time.
   218	
   219	            match const_eval::evaluate_intrinsic(&mut values, intrinsic, &[], input.span()) {
   220	                Ok(Some(value)) => {
   221	                    // Successful evaluation.
   222	                    let expr = self.value_to_expression_node(&value, &input).expect(VALUE_ERROR);
   223	                    return (expr, Some(value));
   224	                }
   225	                Ok(None) =>
   226	                    // No errors, but we were unable to evaluate.
   227	                    {}
   228	                Err(err) => {
   229	                    self.emit_err(StaticAnalyzerError::compile_intrinsic(err, input.span()));
   230	                }
   231	            }
   232	        }
   233	
   234	        (input.into(), Default::default())
   235	    }
   236	
   237	    fn reconstruct_member_access(
   238	        &mut self,
   239	        input: MemberAccess,
   240	        _additional: &(),
   241	    ) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
   242	        let span = input.span();
   243	        let id = input.id();
   244	        let (inner, value_opt) = self.reconstruct_expression(input.inner, &());
   245	        let member_name = input.name.name;
   246	        if let Some(composite) = value_opt {
   247	            let value_result =
   248	                composite.member_access(member_name).expect("Type checking guarantees the member exists.");
   249	
   250	            (self.value_to_expression(&value_result, span, id).expect(VALUE_ERROR), Some(value_result.clone()))
   251	        } else {
   252	            (MemberAccess { inner, ..input }.into(), None)
   253	        }
   254	    }
   255	
   256	    fn reconstruct_repeat(
   257	        &mut self,
   258	        input: leo_ast::RepeatExpression,
   259	        _additional: &(),
   260	    ) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
   261	        let (expr, expr_value) = self.reconstruct_expression(input.expr.clone(), &());
   262	        let (count, count_value) = self.reconstruct_expression(input.count.clone(), &());
   263	
   264	        if count_value.is_none() {
   265	            self.repeat_count_not_evaluated = Some(count.span());
   266	        }
   267	
   268	        match (expr_value, count.as_u32()) {
   269	            (Some(value), Some(count_u32)) => (
   270	                RepeatExpression { expr, count, ..input }.into(),
   271	                Some(Value::make_array(std::iter::repeat_n(value, count_u32 as usize))),
   272	            ),
   273	            _ => (RepeatExpression { expr, count, ..input }.into(), None),
   274	        }
   275	    }
   276	
   277	    fn reconstruct_tuple_access(
   278	        &mut self,
   279	        input: TupleAccess,
   280	        _additional: &(),
   281	    ) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
   282	        let span = input.span();
   283	        let id = input.id();
   284	        let (tuple, value_opt) = self.reconstruct_expression(input.tuple, &());
   285	        if let Some(tuple_value) = value_opt {
   286	            let value_result = tuple_value.tuple_index(input.index.value()).expect("Type checking checked bounds.");
   287	            (self.value_to_expression(&value_result, span, id).expect(VALUE_ERROR), Some(value_result.clone()))
   288	        } else {
   289	            (TupleAccess { tuple, ..input }.into(), None)
   290	        }
   291	    }
   292	
   293	    fn reconstruct_array(
   294	        &mut self,
   295	        mut input: leo_ast::ArrayExpression,
   296	        _additional: &(),
   297	    ) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
   298	        let mut values = Vec::new();
   299	        input.elements.iter_mut().for_each(|element| {
   300	            let (new_element, value_opt) = self.reconstruct_expression(std::mem::take(element), &());
   301	            if let Some(value) = value_opt {
   302	                values.push(value);
   303	            }
   304	            *element = new_element;
   305	        });
   306	        if values.len() == input.elements.len() {
   307	            (input.into(), Some(Value::make_array(values.into_iter())))
   308	        } else {
   309	            (input.into(), None)
   310	        }
   311	    }
   312	
   313	    fn reconstruct_binary(
   314	        &mut self,
   315	        input: leo_ast::BinaryExpression,
   316	        _additional: &(),
   317	    ) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
   318	        let span = input.span();
   319	        let input_id = input.id();
   320	
   321	        let (left, lhs_opt_value) = self.reconstruct_expression(input.left, &());
   322	        let (right, rhs_opt_value) = self.reconstruct_expression(input.right, &());
   323	
   324	        if let (Some(lhs_value), Some(rhs_value)) = (lhs_opt_value, rhs_opt_value) {
   325	            // We were able to evaluate both operands, so we can evaluate this expression.
   326	            match const_eval::evaluate_binary(
   327	                span,
   328	                input.op,
   329	                &lhs_value,
   330	                &rhs_value,
   331	                &self.state.type_table.get(&input_id),
   332	            ) {
   333	                Ok(new_value) => {
   334	                    let new_expr = self.value_to_expression(&new_value, span, input_id).expect(VALUE_ERROR);
   335	                    return (new_expr, Some(new_value));
   336	                }
   337	                Err(err) => self
   338	                    .emit_err(StaticAnalyzerError::compile_time_binary_op(lhs_value, rhs_value, input.op, err, span)),
   339	            }
   340	        }
   341	
   342	        (BinaryExpression { left, right, ..input }.into(), None)
   343	    }
   344	
   345	    fn reconstruct_call(
   346	        &mut self,
   347	        mut input: leo_ast::CallExpression,
   348	        _additional: &(),
   349	    ) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
   350	        input.const_arguments.iter_mut().for_each(|arg| {
   351	            *arg = self.reconstruct_expression(std::mem::take(arg), &()).0;
   352	        });
   353	        input.arguments.iter_mut().for_each(|arg| {
   354	            *arg = self.reconstruct_expression(std::mem::take(arg), &()).0;
   355	        });
   356	        (input.into(), Default::default())
   357	    }
   358	
   359	    fn reconstruct_cast(
   360	        &mut self,
   361	        input: leo_ast::CastExpression,
   362	        _additional: &(),
   363	    ) -> (Expression, Self::AdditionalOutput) {
   364	        let span = input.span();
   365	        let id = input.id();
   366	
   367	        let (expr, opt_value) = self.reconstruct_expression(input.expression, &());
   368

   370	            if let Some(cast_value) = value.cast(&input.type_) {
   371	                let expr = self.value_to_expression(&cast_value, span, id).expect(VALUE_ERROR);
   372	                return (expr, Some(cast_value));
   373	            } else {
   374	                self.emit_err(StaticAnalyzerError::compile_time_cast(value, &input.type_, span))<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you.     17	use super::WriteTransformingVisitor;
    18	use leo_ast::*;
